1a:["$","p",null,{"children":"The entire rendering pipeline consists of six stages:"}]
1b:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Stage 1: React Reconciliation"}]}]
1c:["$","p",null,{"children":["React's reconciler diffs the JSX component tree against the previous frame's Fiber tree, producing a series of DOM operations (create, update, delete nodes). Claude Code uses the ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"react-reconciler"}]," library to create a custom reconciler:"]}]
1e:["$","p",null,{"children":["This reconciler implements methods like ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"createInstance"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"commitUpdate"}],", and ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"removeChild"}],", translating React operations into operations on the Ink DOM tree. Each JSX element type corresponds to an Ink node type:"]}]
20:["$","p",null,{"children":["Note the ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"HostContext"}],"'s ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"isInsideText"}]," field — it prevents nesting ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"<Box>"}]," inside ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"<Text>"}],", which is a fundamental constraint of terminal rendering (text nodes cannot contain block-level layout):"]}]
22:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Stage 2: Yoga Layout Calculation"}]}]
23:["$","p",null,{"children":["Each node in the Ink DOM tree is associated with a Yoga layout node. Yoga is a cross-platform Flexbox layout engine developed by Facebook (originally designed for React Native). Layout calculation is triggered in the reconciler's ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"resetAfterCommit"}],":"]}]
25:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"onComputeLayout"}]," calls Yoga's ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"calculateLayout()"}]," method, computing precise ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"x, y, width, height"}]," for each node — similar to browser CSS Flexbox layout, but with output units in terminal character cells rather than pixels."]}]
26:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Stage 3: Rendering to Output Operations"}]}]
27:["$","p",null,{"children":["After layout is complete, ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"renderNodeToOutput"}]," traverses the Ink DOM tree, transforming each visible node into ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"Output"}]," operations (write, clip, blit, clear, etc.). This stage also handles terminal-specific logic like scrolling, border drawing, and text wrapping:"]}]
29:["$","p",null,{"children":["A key optimization: ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"blit (block transfer)"}],". If a node's position and content haven't changed, the character data for that region is copied directly from the previous frame's Screen buffer, skipping the entire subtree's rendering. This makes steady-state frames (where only a spinner is animating) approach O(changed cells) cost rather than O(total cells)."]}]
2a:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Stage 4: Screen Buffer Generation"}]}]

72:["$","p",null,{"children":"The core virtual scrolling strategies:"}]
73:["$","ol",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":["\n",["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Height estimation"}],": Unmeasured items use ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"DEFAULT_ESTIMATE = 3"}]," lines as an initial estimate. Intentionally biased low — overestimating causes bottom whitespace (premature mount stopping), while underestimating just means mounting a few extra items (absorbed by overscan)."]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":["\n",["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Overscan buffer"}],": 80 extra lines of content are rendered above and below the viewport. Because message heights vary wildly (a tool result could be 100+ lines), a large enough buffer is needed."]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":["\n",["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Scroll quantization"}],": ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"SCROLL_QUANTUM = 40"}]," lines. Triggering a React commit on every scroll wheel tick (3-5 pixels) is unnecessary — as long as the mount range doesn't need to change, visual scrolling is handled by ScrollBox's ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"forceRender"}]," (directly reading the DOM node's scrollTop, bypassing React)."]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":["\n",["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Progressive mounting"}],": ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"SLIDE_STEP = 25"}]," limits each commit to at most 25 new mounted items. This prevents synchronous blocking from mounting 200+ items at once when rapidly scrolling to a completely new area (each MessageRow render takes about 1.5ms)."]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":["\n",["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Render-time clamping"}],": ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"scrollClampMin/Max"}]," constrains scrollTop to the range of mounted content during rendering. When scrollTo writes arrive before React's async re-render, the user sees the edge of mounted content rather than blank space."]}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}]

8c:["$","h2",null,{"children":"Ink's Limitations and Workarounds"}]
8d:["$","h3",null,{"children":"Limitation 1: No Full CSS Capabilities"}]
8e:["$","p",null,{"children":"Terminal Flexbox is only a subset of CSS Flexbox. Unsupported features:"}]
8f:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Grid layout"}],": Only Flexbox, no CSS Grid"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Float/absolute positioning"}],": Yoga's ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"position: absolute"}]," support is limited, and \"absolute positioning\" in the terminal means character-level overwriting"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Percentage heights"}],": Computing percentage heights in scrollable containers would cause layout cycles"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Animation"}],": No CSS transition/animation; all animations are JS-driven (setInterval / requestAnimationFrame)"]}],"\n"]}]
90:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Workarounds"}],":"]}]
91:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":["Use ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"flexDirection"}]," + ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"alignItems"}]," + ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"justifyContent"}]," combinations to simulate most layout needs"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":["Control animations manually through Hooks like ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"useBlink"}]," and ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"useAnimationFrame"}]]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Implement complex layouts (like multi-column options in permission dialogs) with nested Box components"}],"\n"]}]
92:["$","h3",null,{"children":"Limitation 2: Terminal Rendering is Global"}]
93:["$","p",null,{"children":"In a browser, each DOM element renders independently, but a terminal is a global character matrix. This means:"}]
94:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Redraw scope"}],": Any node change can potentially trigger recalculation of the entire Screen"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"z-index simulation"}],": ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"position: absolute"}]," nodes implement \"stacking\" by overwriting characters, but removing them requires marking the entire frame as \"contaminated\", forcing a full redraw"]}],"\n"]}]
96:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Workarounds"}],": The ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"blit"}]," optimization directly copies previous frame data when nodes haven't changed. Layout shift detection tracks node position changes, triggering full redraws only when necessary."]}]
97:["$","h3",null,{"children":"Limitation 3: Inconsistent Character Widths"}]
98:["$","p",null,{"children":"Unicode characters may have different widths in different terminals. CJK characters (Chinese, Japanese, Korean) occupy 2 character widths, emoji may occupy 1 or 2 widths, and some special characters (zero-width joiners, etc.) occupy 0 width."}]
9a:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Workarounds"}],": ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"stringWidth.ts"}]," provides precise Unicode width calculation, and ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"ClusteredChar"}]," pre-computes and caches the width of each grapheme cluster, avoiding repeated calculation in the rendering hot path."]}]
9b:["$","h3",null,{"children":"Limitation 4: ANSI Style Code Conflicts"}]
9c:["$","p",null,{"children":["The shared bold/dim reset code issue mentioned earlier (",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"\\x1b[22m"}],") is a historical defect in the ANSI standard. The chalk library cannot distinguish between ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"</bold>"}]," and ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"</dim>"}]," — closing one closes both simultaneously."]}]
9d:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Workarounds"}],": Avoid mixing bold and dim between adjacent inline elements. When mixing is necessary, separate them with ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"<Box>"}]," (block-level elements reset ANSI state). The ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"minWidth={2}"}]," in ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"ToolUseLoader"}]," is an instance of this strategy."]}]
9e:["$","h3",null,{"children":"Limitation 5: Alt Screen Height Constraint"}]
9f:["$","p",null,{"children":"In Alt Screen mode, content height must exactly equal the terminal row count. If Yoga's calculated height exceeds the terminal rows, cursor positioning becomes corrupted:"}]
a1:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Workarounds"}],": The ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"<AlternateScreen>"}]," component wraps children in ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"<Box height={rows} flexShrink={0}>"}],", forcing height to equal the terminal row count. Overflowing content is silently clipped, and a warning log is emitted."]}]
a2:["$","h2",null,{"children":"Portable Patterns"}]
a3:["$","p",null,{"children":"Claude Code's terminal UI architecture contains several patterns worth adopting in other CLI projects:"}]
a4:["$","h3",null,{"children":"Pattern 1: Renderless Components"}]
a5:["$","p",null,{"children":["Encapsulate interaction logic as React components that return ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"null"}],":"]}]
a7:["$","p",null,{"children":"Advantages:"}]
a8:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Enjoy React's lifecycle management (automatic event listener cleanup)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Composable (render in parallel with other components)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":["Conditionally renderable (via ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"isActive"}]," or ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"{condition && <Handler />}"}],")"]}],"\n"]}]
a9:["$","h3",null,{"children":"Pattern 2: Double Buffering + Frame Diffing"}]
aa:["$","p",null,{"children":"Maintain two Screen buffers, writing only changed cells to the terminal each frame:"}]
ac:["$","p",null,{"children":"This makes steady-state rendering (where only a spinner is changing) approach O(1) cost, rather than O(rows * cols)."}]
ad:["$","h3",null,{"children":"Pattern 3: Virtual Scrolling + Progressive Mounting"}]
ae:["$","p",null,{"children":"For long conversations that may contain hundreds of messages:"}]
af:["$","ol",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":["Only mount messages near the viewport (",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"useVirtualScroll"}],")"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Fill unmounted areas with spacers"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Progressively mount during rapid scrolling (max 25 items per frame)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Render-time clamping to prevent blank flashes"}],"\n"]}]
b0:["$","h3",null,{"children":"Pattern 4: Suspense Async Data Loading"}]
b1:["$","p",null,{"children":["Use ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"useState(() => promise)"}]," + ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"use(promise)"}]," + ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"<Suspense>"}]," for async data:"]}]
b3:["$","p",null,{"children":"This shows a placeholder while data loads, then automatically replaces it when complete — identical to Suspense usage in the browser."}]
b4:["$","h3",null,{"children":"Pattern 5: Double-Press Confirmation for Destructive Actions"}]
b5:["$","p",null,{"children":"For irreversible actions (like terminating all background agents), use time-windowed double confirmation:"}]
b7:["$","h3",null,{"children":"Pattern 6: Pooled String Interning"}]
b8:["$","p",null,{"children":"For strings that need frequent comparison (characters, styles, hyperlinks), use an intern pool to map strings to integer IDs:"}]
ba:["$","p",null,{"children":["Inter-frame diff comparison becomes integer comparison (",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"==="}],") rather than string comparison, yielding significant performance gains at the millions-of-operations scale."]}]
bb:["$","h2",null,{"children":"Summary"}]
bc:["$","p",null,{"children":["Claude Code's terminal UI architecture showcases a deeply customized React terminal rendering solution. From the custom ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"react-reconciler"}]," host config, to the Yoga layout engine, double-buffered Screen diffing, virtual scrolling, and through to 140+ business components and 85 Hooks — it is one of the most complex terminal React applications known."]}]
bd:["$","p",null,{"children":"Key takeaways:"}]
be:["$","ol",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Rendering pipeline"}],": JSX -> React Reconcile -> Ink DOM -> Yoga Layout -> Screen Buffer -> ANSI diff -> stdout. A six-stage pipeline where blit optimization makes steady-state frames approach zero cost"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Component architecture"}],": Foundation layer (Box/Text/ScrollBox) + Application layer (Message/Permission/Diff/Spinner), with message routing dispatching by type to dedicated rendering components"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Performance strategies"}],": Markdown token LRU cache, virtual scroll progressive mounting, string pool interning, scroll quantization to reduce React commits"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Interaction patterns"}],": Renderless components for shortcut logic, multi-priority cancellation chain, time-window double confirmation"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Limitation mitigation"}],": bold/dim ANSI code conflict isolation with Box, Alt Screen height forced clamping, absolute node removal marking full-frame contamination"]}],"\n"]}]
bf:["$","p",null,{"children":["This architecture proves an important point: ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"React's value lies not just in DOM rendering, but in its declarative programming model and component-based architecture"}],". After switching the render target to a terminal character matrix, React's state management, lifecycle, Hooks, Suspense and other core capabilities remain perfectly applicable — and these are precisely the capabilities needed to build complex interactive CLI applications."]}]
